## Tool | Trade Up Contract (id: 12032)


### Translation Changes

#### Before

```javascript
{
  desc: "In exchange for 10 items of identical quality, you will receive a single item of a quality one higher, from a collection of one of the items you provided."
}
```
#### After

```javascript
{
  desc: "In exchange for several items of identical quality, you will receive a single item of a quality one higher, from a collection of one of the items you provided."
}
```
